\documentclass[11pt]{article}

    \usepackage[breakable]{tcolorbox}
    \usepackage{parskip} % Stop auto-indenting (to mimic markdown behaviour)
    

    % Basic figure setup, for now with no caption control since it's done
    % automatically by Pandoc (which extracts ![](path) syntax from Markdown).
    \usepackage{graphicx}
    % Maintain compatibility with old templates. Remove in nbconvert 6.0
    \let\Oldincludegraphics\includegraphics
    % Ensure that by default, figures have no caption (until we provide a
    % proper Figure object with a Caption API and a way to capture that
    % in the conversion process - todo).
    \usepackage{caption}
    \DeclareCaptionFormat{nocaption}{}
    \captionsetup{format=nocaption,aboveskip=0pt,belowskip=0pt}

    \usepackage{float}
    \floatplacement{figure}{H} % forces figures to be placed at the correct location
    \usepackage{xcolor} % Allow colors to be defined
    \usepackage{enumerate} % Needed for markdown enumerations to work
    \usepackage{geometry} % Used to adjust the document margins
    \usepackage{amsmath} % Equations
    \usepackage{amssymb} % Equations
    \usepackage{textcomp} % defines textquotesingle
    % Hack from http://tex.stackexchange.com/a/47451/13684:
    \AtBeginDocument{%
        \def\PYZsq{\textquotesingle}% Upright quotes in Pygmentized code
    }
    \usepackage{upquote} % Upright quotes for verbatim code
    \usepackage{eurosym} % defines \euro

    \usepackage{iftex}
    \ifPDFTeX
        \usepackage[T1]{fontenc}
        \IfFileExists{alphabeta.sty}{
              \usepackage{alphabeta}
          }{
              \usepackage[mathletters]{ucs}
              \usepackage[utf8x]{inputenc}
          }
    \else
        \usepackage{fontspec}
        \usepackage{unicode-math}
    \fi

    \usepackage{fancyvrb} % verbatim replacement that allows latex
    \usepackage{grffile} % extends the file name processing of package graphics
                         % to support a larger range
    \makeatletter % fix for old versions of grffile with XeLaTeX
    \@ifpackagelater{grffile}{2019/11/01}
    {
      % Do nothing on new versions
    }
    {
      \def\Gread@@xetex#1{%
        \IfFileExists{"\Gin@base".bb}%
        {\Gread@eps{\Gin@base.bb}}%
        {\Gread@@xetex@aux#1}%
      }
    }
    \makeatother
    \usepackage[Export]{adjustbox} % Used to constrain images to a maximum size
    \adjustboxset{max size={0.9\linewidth}{0.9\paperheight}}

    % The hyperref package gives us a pdf with properly built
    % internal navigation ('pdf bookmarks' for the table of contents,
    % internal cross-reference links, web links for URLs, etc.)
    \usepackage{hyperref}
    % The default LaTeX title has an obnoxious amount of whitespace. By default,
    % titling removes some of it. It also provides customization options.
    \usepackage{titling}
    \usepackage{longtable} % longtable support required by pandoc >1.10
    \usepackage{booktabs}  % table support for pandoc > 1.12.2
    \usepackage{array}     % table support for pandoc >= 2.11.3
    \usepackage{calc}      % table minipage width calculation for pandoc >= 2.11.1
    \usepackage[inline]{enumitem} % IRkernel/repr support (it uses the enumerate* environment)
    \usepackage[normalem]{ulem} % ulem is needed to support strikethroughs (\sout)
                                % normalem makes italics be italics, not underlines
    \usepackage{soul}      % strikethrough (\st) support for pandoc >= 3.0.0
    \usepackage{mathrsfs}

    % For linebreaks inside Verbatim environment from package fancyvrb.
    \makeatletter
        \newbox\Wrappedcontinuationbox
        \newbox\Wrappedvisiblespacebox
        \newcommand*\Wrappedvisiblespace {\textcolor{red}{\textvisiblespace}}
        \newcommand*\Wrappedcontinuationsymbol {\textcolor{red}{\llap{\tiny$\m@th\hookrightarrow$}}}
        \newcommand*\Wrappedcontinuationindent {3ex }
        \newcommand*\Wrappedafterbreak {\kern\Wrappedcontinuationindent\copy\Wrappedcontinuationbox}
        % Take advantage of the already applied Pygments mark-up to insert
        % potential linebreaks for TeX processing.
        %        {, <, #, %, $, ' and ": go to next line.
        %        _, }, ^, &, >, - and ~: stay at end of broken line.
        % Use of \textquotesingle for straight quote.
        \newcommand*\Wrappedbreaksatspecials {%
            \def\PYGZus{\discretionary{\char`\_}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\_}}%
            \def\PYGZob{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\{}{\char`\{}}%
            \def\PYGZcb{\discretionary{\char`\}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\}}}%
            \def\PYGZca{\discretionary{\char`\^}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\^}}%
            \def\PYGZam{\discretionary{\char`\&}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\&}}%
            \def\PYGZlt{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\<}{\char`\<}}%
            \def\PYGZgt{\discretionary{\char`\>}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\>}}%
            \def\PYGZsh{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\#}{\char`\#}}%
            \def\PYGZpc{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\%}{\char`\%}}%
            \def\PYGZdl{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\$}{\char`\$}}%
            \def\PYGZhy{\discretionary{\char`\-}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\-}}%
            \def\PYGZsq{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\textquotesingle}{\textquotesingle}}%
            \def\PYGZdq{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\"}{\char`\"}}%
            \def\PYGZti{\discretionary{\char`\~}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\~}}%
        }
        % Some characters . , ; ? ! / are not pygmentized.
        % This macro makes them "active" and they will insert potential linebreaks
        \newcommand*\Wrappedbreaksatpunct {%
            \lccode`\~`\.\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\.}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\.}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\,\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\,}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\,}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\;\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\;}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\;}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\:\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\:}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\:}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\?\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\?}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\?}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\!\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\!}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\!}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\/\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\/}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\/}}}%
            \catcode`\.\active
            \catcode`\,\active
            \catcode`\;\active
            \catcode`\:\active
            \catcode`\?\active
            \catcode`\!\active
            \catcode`\/\active
            \lccode`\~`\~
        }
    \makeatother

    \let\OriginalVerbatim=\Verbatim
    \makeatletter
    \renewcommand{\Verbatim}[1][1]{%
        %\parskip\z@skip
        \sbox\Wrappedcontinuationbox {\Wrappedcontinuationsymbol}%
        \sbox\Wrappedvisiblespacebox {\FV@SetupFont\Wrappedvisiblespace}%
        \def\FancyVerbFormatLine ##1{\hsize\linewidth
            \vtop{\raggedright\hyphenpenalty\z@\exhyphenpenalty\z@
                \doublehyphendemerits\z@\finalhyphendemerits\z@
                \strut ##1\strut}%
        }%
        % If the linebreak is at a space, the latter will be displayed as visible
        % space at end of first line, and a continuation symbol starts next line.
        % Stretch/shrink are however usually zero for typewriter font.
        \def\FV@Space {%
            \nobreak\hskip\z@ plus\fontdimen3\font minus\fontdimen4\font
            \discretionary{\copy\Wrappedvisiblespacebox}{\Wrappedafterbreak}
            {\kern\fontdimen2\font}%
        }%

        % Allow breaks at special characters using \PYG... macros.
        \Wrappedbreaksatspecials
        % Breaks at punctuation characters . , ; ? ! and / need catcode=\active
        \OriginalVerbatim[#1,codes*=\Wrappedbreaksatpunct]%
    }
    \makeatother

    \definecolor{outcolor}{HTML}{D84315}
    \definecolor{cellborder}{HTML}{CFCFCF}
    \definecolor{cellbackground}{HTML}{F7F7F7}

    % prompt
    \makeatletter
    \newcommand{\boxspacing}{\kern\kvtcb@left@rule\kern\kvtcb@boxsep}
    \makeatother
    \newcommand{\prompt}[4]{
        {\ttfamily\llap{{\color{#2}[#3]:\hspace{3pt}#4}}\vspace{-\baselineskip}}
    }
    

    
    % Prevent overflowing lines due to hard-to-break entities
    \sloppy
    % Setup hyperref package
    \hypersetup{
      breaklinks=true,  % so long urls are correctly broken across lines
      colorlinks=true,
      urlcolor=urlcolor,
      linkcolor=linkcolor,
      citecolor=citecolor,
      }
    % Slightly bigger margins than the latex defaults
    
    \geometry{verbose,tmargin=1in,bmargin=1in,lmargin=1in,rmargin=1in}
    
    

\begin{document}
    
    \maketitle
    
    

    
    \hypertarget{analysing-router-logs}{%
\section{Analysing Router Logs}\label{analysing-router-logs}}

We will first import necessary libraries

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{1}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{pandas} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n+nn}{pd}
\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{numpy} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n+nn}{np}

    \hypertarget{strategy}{%
\subsection{Strategy}\label{strategy}}

\begin{enumerate}
\def\labelenumi{\arabic{enumi}.}
\tightlist
\item
  We will try and simluate a few attacks on a router, and check whether
  those attacks can be detected in hindsight.
\item
  To do that we will start with generating some demo data for a router,
  inspired by my home router. This will be a monitor of active DHCP
  Clients.
\item
  We will then try and analyse the data to find out anomalies in normal
  usage.
\end{enumerate}

    \hypertarget{generating-normal-demo-data}{%

data}{Generating normal demo data}}\label{generating-normal-demo-data}}

\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{generate\PYZus{}dest\PYZus{}ip\PYZus{}address}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} define the weights for each website}
    \PY{n}{website\PYZus{}weights} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Youtube}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{15}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Instagram}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Facebook}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{8}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Twitter}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Other}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} create a list of websites based on their weights}
    \PY{n}{websites} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{website}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{weight} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{website\PYZus{}weights}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{items}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{websites}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{extend}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{website}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{weight}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} randomly select a website from the list}
    \PY{n}{website} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{random}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{choice}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{websites}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} generate a random IP address for the website}
    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{website} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Youtube}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k}{return} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{216.58.194.45}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}} \PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{website}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{elif} \PY{n}{website} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Instagram}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k}{return} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{3.213.31.34}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}} \PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{website}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{elif} \PY{n}{website} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Facebook}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k}{return} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{69.63.176.22}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}} \PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{website}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{elif} \PY{n}{website} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Twitter}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k}{return} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{104.244.42.12}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}} \PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{website}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{generate\PYZus{}device\PYZus{}ip\PYZus{}address}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} define a list of 10 predefined IP addresses}
    \PY{n}{ips} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{192.168.1.10}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{192.168.1.20}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{192.168.1.30}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{192.168.1.40}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{192.168.1.50}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} generate a random integer between 0 and 9}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} return the IP address at the selected index}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{ips}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{generate\PYZus{}device\PYZus{}name}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{device\PYZus{}names} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{iPhone}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Samsung}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{OnePlus}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Nokia}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Xiaomi}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Oppo}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Vivo}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Realme}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Micromax}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Lenovo}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{generate\PYZus{}interface}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}

    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{random}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{choice}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{interfaces}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{generate\PYZus{}date\PYZus{}time}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} generate random date and time, but only in the range of a few days}
    \PY{n}{start\PYZus{}date} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to\PYZus{}datetime}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{2023\PYZhy{}01\PYZhy{}01}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} generate random number of days}
    \PY{n}{days\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}add} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{random}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{randint}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} generate random number of seconds}
    \PY{n}{seconds\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}add} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{random}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{randint}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{86400}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} add random days and seconds to start date}
    \PY{n}{end\PYZus{}date} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{start\PYZus{}date} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{Timedelta}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{days}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{days\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}add}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{seconds}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{seconds\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}add}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} set the hour of the timestamp based on the time of day}
    \PY{n}{hour} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{end\PYZus{}date}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{hour}
    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{hour} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{6}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} almost no traffic between 2am and 6am}
        \PY{n}{hour} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{random}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{randint}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{6}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{23}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{elif} \PY{n}{hour} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{9}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} more traffic during the morning hours}
        \PY{n}{hour} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{random}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{randint}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{6}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{elif} \PY{n}{hour} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{18}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} most traffic during the daytime}
        \PY{n}{hour} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{random}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{randint}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{9}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{17}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} less traffic during the evening hours}
        \PY{n}{hour} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{random}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{randint}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{17}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{23}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} set the hour of the timestamp}
    \PY{n}{end\PYZus{}date} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{end\PYZus{}date}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{replace}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{hour}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{hour}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} return timestamp as string}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{end\PYZus{}date}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{strftime}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Y\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{m\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZpc{}d}\PY{l+s+s1}{ }\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{H:}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{M:}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{S}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{gen\PYZus{}protocols}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{protocols} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{TCP}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{UDP}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{DHCP}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{HTTP}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{HTTPS}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{FTP}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{SMTP}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{POP3}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{IMAP}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{DNS}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{ICMP}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{n}{ports} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}
        \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{TCP}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{21}\PY{p}{,}          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} HTTP}
        \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{UDP}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{53}\PY{p}{,}          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} DNS}
        \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{DHCP}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{67}\PY{p}{,}         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} DHCP Server}
        \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{HTTP}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{80}\PY{p}{,}         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Hypertext Transfer Protocol}
        \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{HTTPS}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{443}\PY{p}{,}       \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} HTTP Secure (TLS/SSL)}
        \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{FTP}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{21}\PY{p}{,}          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} File Transfer Protocol (Control)}
        \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{SMTP}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{25}\PY{p}{,}         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Simple Mail Transfer Protocol}
        \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{POP3}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{110}\PY{p}{,}        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Post Office Protocol v3}
        \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{IMAP}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{143}\PY{p}{,}        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Internet Message Access Protocol}
        \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{DNS}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{53}\PY{p}{,}          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Domain Name System}

\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{generate\PYZus{}date\PYZus{}time}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} generate random date and time, but only in the range of a few days}
    \PY{n}{start\PYZus{}date} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to\PYZus{}datetime}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{2023\PYZhy{}01\PYZhy{}01}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} generate random number of seconds}
    \PY{n}{seconds\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}add} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{random}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{randint}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{86400}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} add random days and seconds to start date}
    \PY{n}{end\PYZus{}date} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{start\PYZus{}date} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{Timedelta}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{days}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{days\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}add}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{seconds}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{seconds\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}add}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} set the hour of the timestamp based on the time of day}
    \PY{n}{hour} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{end\PYZus{}date}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{hour}
    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{hour} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{6}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} almost no traffic between 2am and 6am}
        \PY{n}{hour} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{random}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{randint}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{6}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{23}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{elif} \PY{n}{hour} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{9}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} more traffic during the morning hours}
        \PY{n}{hour} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{random}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{randint}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{6}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{elif} \PY{n}{hour} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{18}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} most traffic during the daytime}
        \PY{n}{hour} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{random}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{randint}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{9}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{17}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} less traffic during the evening hours}
        \PY{n}{hour} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{random}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{randint}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{17}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{23}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} set the hour of the timestamp}
    \PY{n}{end\PYZus{}date} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{end\PYZus{}date}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{replace}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{hour}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{hour}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} return timestamp as string}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{end\PYZus{}date}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{strftime}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Y\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{m\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZpc{}d}\PY{l+s+s1}{ }\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{H:}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{M:}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{S}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\subsection{Port Scanning}\label{port-scanning}}

This is a surveillance technique that is used to identify open ports on
a system. This is used by hackers to identify vulnerable ports on a
system.

\PY{n}{subtitle} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{A general rise in requests is visible between Wednesday and Sunday, indicating a possible port scanning attack.}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}

\PY{p}{)}
